**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "function Invoke-DissolveAnimation {\n    <#\n    .SYNOPSIS\n        Cow materializes character by character in random positions.\n    .DESCRIPTION\n        Creates a \"teleportation\" or \"materialization\" effect — characters\n        appear randomly across the canvas until the full cow is revealed.\n        Each frame adds more characters, building up from noise to clarity.\n        Uses cursor repositioning for smooth, flicker-free rendering.\n    #>\n    [CmdletBinding()]\n    [Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis.SuppressMessageAttribute('PSAvoidUsingWriteHost', '')]\n    [Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis.SuppressMessageAttribute('PSReviewUnusedParameter', 'Message')]\n    param(\n        [Parameter(Mandatory)]\n        [string]$CowOutput,\n\n        [string]$Message = '',\n\n        [ValidateRange(1, 20)]\n        [int]$Speed = 5,\n\n        [ValidateRange(3, 100)]\n        [int]$Duration = 15\n    )\n\n    $lines = $CowOutput -split \"`n\"\n    $maxLen = 0\n    foreach ($line in $lines) {\n        if ($line.Length -gt $maxLen) { $maxLen = $line.Length }\n    }\n    $lineCount = $lines.Count\n\n    # Pad all lines to equal length\n    $paddedLines = @()\n    foreach ($line in $lines) {\n        $paddedLines += $line.PadRight($maxLen)\n    }\n\n    # Build character grid as nested arrays (PS 5.1 compatible)\n    $charGrid = @()\n    for ($r = 0; $r -lt $lineCount; $r++) {\n        $row = @()\n        for ($c = 0; $c -lt $maxLen; $c++) {\n            $row += $paddedLines[$r][$c]\n        }\n        $charGrid += ,$row\n    }\n\n    # Create shuffled list of all positions\n    $totalChars = $lineCount * $maxLen\n    $positions = @()\n    for ($i = 0; $i -lt $totalChars; $i++) {\n        $positions += $i\n    }\n    # Fisher-Yates shuffle\n    for ($i = $positions.Count - 1; $i -gt 0; $i--) {\n        $j = Get-Random -Minimum 0 -Maximum ($i + 1)\n        $temp = $positions[$i]\n        $positions[$i] = $positions[$j]\n        $positions[$j] = $temp\n    }\n\n    $charsPerFrame = [Math]::Max(1, [Math]::Ceiling($totalChars / $Duration))\n    $revealedCount = 0\n\n    # Display grid — starts as spaces\n    $displayGrid = @()\n    for ($r = 0; $r -lt $lineCount; $r++) {\n        $row = @()\n        for ($c = 0; $c -lt $maxLen; $c++) {\n            $row += ' '\n        }\n        $displayGrid += ,$row\n    }\n\n    $sb = [System.Text.StringBuilder]::new($maxLen * $lineCount * 2)\n\n    for ($frame = 0; $frame -lt $Duration; $frame++) {\n        # Reveal characters for this frame\n        for ($s = 0; $s -lt $charsPerFrame -and $revealedCount -lt $totalChars; $s++) {\n            $pos = $positions[$revealedCount]\n            $r = [Math]::Floor($pos / $maxLen)\n            $c = $pos % $maxLen\n            $displayGrid[$r][$c] = $charGrid[$r][$c]\n            $revealedCount++\n        }\n\n        # Build display string\n        [void]$sb.Clear()\n        for ($r = 0; $r -lt $lineCount; $r++) {\n            if ($r -gt 0) { [void]$sb.AppendLine() }\n            for ($c = 0; $c -lt $maxLen; $c++) {\n                [void]$sb.Append($displayGrid[$r][$c])\n            }\n        }\n\n        try {\n            if ($frame -gt 0 -and [Console]::CursorTop -ge $lineCount) {\n                [Console]::SetCursorPosition(0, [Console]::CursorTop - $lineCount)\n            }\n            Write-Host $sb.ToString() -NoNewline\n        } catch {\n            Write-Host $sb.ToString()\n        }\n\n        Start-Sleep -Milliseconds 40\n    }\n\n    Write-Host \"\"\n    return $CowOutput\n}\n",

}
```

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "function Invoke-BlinkAnimation {\n    <#\n    .SYNOPSIS\n        Cow eyes blink periodically while displaying.\n    .DESCRIPTION\n        Shows the cow with normal eyes, then periodically replaces them\n        with closed-eye characters (- -) for a natural blink effect.\n        Creates a living, breathing feel. Uses cursor repositioning\n        for smooth frame transitions without screen flicker.\n    #>\n    [CmdletBinding()]\n    [Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis.SuppressMessageAttribute('PSAvoidUsingWriteHost', '')]\n    [Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis.SuppressMessageAttribute('PSReviewUnusedParameter', 'Message')]\n    param(\n        [Parameter(Mandatory)]\n        [string]$CowOutput,\n\n        [string]$Message = '',\n\n        [ValidateRange(1, 100)]\n        [int]$Duration = 15,\n\n        [ValidateRange(0.05, 0.8)]\n        [double]$BlinkRate = 0.2\n    )\n\n    $lines = $CowOutput -split \"`n\"\n\n    # Find lines containing eye patterns (parenthesized 2-char expressions)\n    $eyeLineIndices = @()\n    $originalEyeLines = @()\n\n    for ($i = 0; $i -lt $lines.Count; $i++) {\n        if ($lines[$i] -match '\\([^)]{2}\\)') {\n            $eyeLineIndices += $i\n            $originalEyeLines += $lines[$i]\n        }\n    }\n\n    # Create closed-eye versions (replace eyes with dashes)\n    $closedEyeLines = @()\n    foreach ($line in $originalEyeLines) {\n        $closedEyeLines += ($line -replace '\\(([^)]{2})\\)', '(- -)')\n    }\n\n    $sb = [System.Text.StringBuilder]::new($CowOutput.Length * 2)\n\n    try { $startTop = [Console]::CursorTop } catch { $startTop = 0 }\n\n    for ($frame = 0; $frame -lt $Duration; $frame++) {\n        [void]$sb.Clear()\n\n        # Determine if this frame is a blink\n        $isBlink = ($frame -eq 3) -or ($frame -eq 10)\n\n        for ($i = 0; $i -lt $lines.Count; $i++) {\n            if ($i -gt 0) { [void]$sb.AppendLine() }\n\n            $eyeIdx = -1\n            for ($e = 0; $e -lt $eyeLineIndices.Count; $e++) {\n                if ($eyeLineIndices[$e] -eq $i) { $eyeIdx = $e; break }\n            }\n\n            if ($eyeIdx -ge 0 -and $isBlink) {\n                [void]$sb.Append($closedEyeLines[$eyeIdx])\n            } else {\n                [void]$sb.Append($lines[$i])\n            }\n        }\n\n        try {\n            if ($frame -gt 0 -and [Console]::CursorTop -ge $lines.Count) {\n                [Console]::SetCursorPosition(0, [Console]::CursorTop - $lines.Count)\n            }\n            Write-Host $sb.ToString() -NoNewline\n        } catch {\n            Write-Host $sb.ToString()\n        }\n\n        Start-Sleep -Milliseconds 200\n    }\n\n    Write-Host \"\"\n    return $CowOutput\n}\n",
  "filePath": "D:\\Projects\\Forgum\\Private\\Animation\\Blink.ps1"
}
```

## Assistant (Build · MiMo V2.5 Free · 9.6s)

_Thinking:_

All done! Let me provide a summary.

Done. Here's the summary:

## 8 New Animation Modes Added

| Mode | Effect |
|------|--------|
| `slide-in` | Cow slides in from left, column by column |
| `bounce` | Cow drops in with realistic bounce physics |
| `dissolve` | Cow materializes character by character randomly |
| `fade-in` | Cow fades in line by line with brightness |
| `blink` | Cow eyes blink periodically |
| `wiggle` | Cow wiggles left and right playfully |
| `wave` | Fortune text appears word by word with rainbow |
| `disco` | Cow cycles through rainbow colors (party mode) |

**Stats:**
- **161/161 tests passing**
- **12 files changed** (941 lines added)
- **All animations** use cursor repositioning for smooth, video-like rendering
- **Committed & pushed** to GitHub + GitLab

**Try it:**
```powershell
$config = Get-CFConfig
$config.animation.mode = 'disco'   # or 'bounce', 'dissolve', 'blink', etc.
Set-CFConfig -Config $config
Invoke-Forgum
```

```
354:     It "produces colored output when enabled with all options" {

356:         $config = Get-CFConfig
357:         $config.lolcat.enabled = $true
358:         $config.lolcat.truecolor = $true

360:         $config.lolcat.invert = $false

364:         $config.animation.mode = 'static'

367:         $output = Invoke-Forgum -Think -CowFile 'default' -Eyes '@@'

372:         $stripped | Should -Match '@@'
373:         $stripped | Should -Match '\^__\^'

379:     }

392:         $esc = [char]27
```

```json
{
  "filePath": "D:\\Projects\\Forgum\\Tests\\Comprehensive.Tests.ps1"
```

```
<content>
1: #Requires -Modules Pester
2: 
3: # Prevent auto-start from modifying config during tests
4: $env:FORGUM_NOAUTOSTART = '1'
5: 
6: Describe "Comprehensive Feature Matrix Tests" {
7:     BeforeAll {
8:         $modulePath = Join-Path (Split-Path $PSScriptRoot -Parent) 'Forgum.psd1'
9:         Import-Module $modulePath -Force
10:         $script:OriginalConfig = Get-Content (Join-Path (Split-Path $PSScriptRoot -Parent) 'Data/Templates/default-config.json') -Raw | ConvertFrom-Json
11:         Set-CFConfig -Config $script:OriginalConfig

13: 
14:     AfterAll {
15:         Set-CFConfig -Config $script:OriginalConfig
16:     }
17: 
18:     AfterEach {
19:         Set-CFConfig -Config $script:OriginalConfig
20:     }
21: 
22:     # --- TEST 1: Invoke-Cowsay with default params returns string with cow face ---
23:     It "Test 01: Invoke-Cowsay default returns string containing cow face" {
24:         $output = Invoke-Cowsay -Text "Hello"
25:         $output | Should -BeOfType System.String
26:         $raw = $output -replace '\x1b\[[0-9;]*[a-zA-Z]', ''
27:         $raw | Should -Match '\^__\^'
28:     }
29: 
30:     # --- TEST 2: Invoke-Cowsay with all params (Text, CowFile, Eyes, Tongue, Thoughts) ---
31:     It "Test 02: Invoke-Cowsay with all custom params applies all substitutions" {
32:         $output = Invoke-Cowsay -Text "CustomAll" -CowFile 'tux' -Eyes '@@' -Tongue '##' -Thoughts 'o'
33:         $raw = $output -replace '\x1b\[[0-9;]*[a-zA-Z]', ''
34:         $raw | Should -Match 'CustomAll'
```

```
229:         $output = Invoke-Cowsay -Text 'Anything'
230:         $raw = $output -replace '\x1b\[[0-9;]*[a-zA-Z]', ''
231:         $raw | Should -Match '\^__\^'
232:     }
233: 
234:     It "Ghost 28: Speech balloon borders are properly closed" {
235:         $output = Invoke-Cowsay -Text 'Test'
236:         $raw = $output -replace '\x1b\[[0-9;]*[a-zA-Z]', ''
237:         $lines = $raw -split "`n"
238:         # Find lines that are all # (with optional leading spaces)
239:         $hashLines = $lines | Where-Object { $_.Trim() -match '^#+$' }
240:         $hashLines.Count | Should -BeGreaterOrEqual 2
241:         # First and last hash lines should have same length
242:         $hashLines[0].Trim().Length | Should -Be $hashLines[-1].Trim().Length
243:     }
244: 
245:     It "Ghost 29: Think bubble uses o not backslash" {
246:         $output = Invoke-Cowsay -Text 'Think' -Thoughts 'o'
247:         $raw = $output -replace '\x1b\[[0-9;]*[a-zA-Z]', ''
248:         # Should have 'o' connector, not '\'
249:         $raw | Should -Match 'o\s+\^__\^'
250:         $raw | Should -Not -Match '\\\s+\^__\^'
251:     }
252: 
253:     It "Ghost 30: Invoke-Forgum returns complete cow with fortune" {
254:         $output = Invoke-Forgum
255:         $output | Should -Not -BeNullOrEmpty

257:         # Should have balloon, cow face, and fortune text
258:         $raw | Should -Match '\^__\^'
259:         $raw | Should -Match '#'
260:         $raw | Should -Match '\|\|'
261:     }
262: }
263:

265:     BeforeAll {
266:         Import-Module (Join-Path (Split-Path $PSScriptRoot -Parent) 'Forgum.psd1') -Force
267:         $script:ProjectRoot = Split-Path $PSScriptRoot -Parent
268:     }
269: 
270:     It "no Invoke-Expression in public functions" {
271:         $publicFiles = Get-ChildItem "$script:ProjectRoot/Public/*.ps1"
272:         foreach ($f in $publicFiles) {
273:             $content = Get-Content $f.FullName -Raw
274:             $content | Should -Not -Match 'Invoke-Expression'
275:         }
276:     }
277: 
278:     It "no Invoke-Expression in private functions" {
279:         $privateFiles = Get-ChildItem "$script:ProjectRoot/Private/*.ps1" -Recurse
280:         foreach ($f in $privateFiles) {
281:             $content = Get-Content $f.FullName -Raw
282:             $content | Should -Not -Match 'Invoke-Expression'
283:         }
284:     }
285: 
286:     It "config loads without error" {
287:         { Get-CFConfig -ErrorAction Stop } | Should -Not -Throw
288:     }
289: 
290:     It "all .cow files are safe (no executable content)" {
291:         $cowFiles = Get-ChildItem "$script:ProjectRoot/Data/Cows/*.cow" -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue
292:         foreach ($f in $cowFiles) {
293:             $content = Get-Content $f.FullName -Raw
294:             $content | Should -Not -Match 'Invoke-Expression|Invoke-Command|Start-Process'
295:         }
```

```
1: function Get-CFConfig {
2:     <#
3:     .SYNOPSIS
4:         Returns the current Forgum configuration.
5:     .DESCRIPTION
6:         Loads config from disk (with caching) or returns defaults.
7:         Config is cached for 30 seconds to avoid repeated disk reads.
8:     .EXAMPLE
9:         Get-CFConfig
10:         Returns the full configuration object.
11:     .EXAMPLE
12:         (Get-CFConfig).lolcat.enabled
13:         Returns just the lolcat enabled setting.
14:     #>
15:     [CmdletBinding()]
16:     [OutputType([PSCustomObject])]
17:     param()
18: 
19:     # Return cached config if still valid
20:     $now = [datetime]::UtcNow
21:     if ($null -ne $script:ConfigCache -and
22:         ($now - $script:ConfigCacheTime).TotalSeconds -lt $script:ConfigCacheTTL) {
23:         return $script:ConfigCache
24:     }
25: 
26:     $path = Get-ConfigPath
27: 
28:     if (Test-Path $path) {
29:         try {
30:             $config = Get-Content $path -Raw -ErrorAction Stop | ConvertFrom-Json -ErrorAction Stop
31:         }
32:         catch {
33:             Write-Warning "Forgum: Corrupt config file, using defaults. Error: $($_.Exception.Message)"
34:             $config = $null
35:         }
36:     }
37: 
38:     if (-not $config) {
39:         $defaultPath = Join-Path (Split-Path $PSScriptRoot -Parent) 'Data/Templates/default-config.json'
40:         if (-not (Test-Path $defaultPath)) {
41:             $defaultPath = Join-Path $PSScriptRoot 'Data/Templates/default-config.json'
42:         }
43:         $config = Get-Content $defaultPath -Raw -ErrorAction Stop | ConvertFrom-Json -ErrorAction Stop
44:     }
45: 
46:     # Ensure all required sections exist with defaults
47:     $required = @{
48:         animation = @{ mode = 'static'; speed = 20; duration = 12; spread = 3.0 }
49:         cow = @{ file = 'default'; random = $false; mode = $null; eyes = 'oo'; tongue = '  ' }
50:         fortune = @{ database = 'fortunes'; offensive = $false }
51:         lolcat = @{ enabled = $false; truecolor = $true; frequency = 0.1; spread = 3.0; seed = 0; invert = $false; animate = $false; duration = 12; speed = 20.0 }
52:         output = @{ wordWrap = $true; maxWidth = 60 }
53:         startup = @{ enabled = $true; command = 'Invoke-Forgum' }
54:         shell = @{ integration = 'auto'; tmux = @{ enabled = $false; pane = 'status-right' } }
55:     }
56:     foreach ($key in $required.Keys) {
57:         if (-not $config.PSObject.Properties[$key] -or $null -eq $config.$key) {
58:             $config | Add-Member -NotePropertyName $key -NotePropertyValue ($required[$key] | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 5 | ConvertFrom-Json) -Force
59:         }
60:         foreach ($subKey in $required[$key].Keys) {
61:             if (-not $config.$key.PSObject.Properties[$subKey] -or $null -eq $config.$key.$subKey) {
62:                 $config.$key | Add-Member -NotePropertyName $subKey -NotePropertyValue $required[$key][$subKey] -Force
63:             }
64:         }
65:     }
66: 
67:     # Cache the result
68:     $script:ConfigCache = $config
69:     $script:ConfigCacheTime = $now
70: 
71:     return $config
72: }

(End of file - total 72 lines)
</content>
```

```
1: function Set-CFConfig {
2:     <#
3:     .SYNOPSIS
4:         Saves the Forgum configuration to disk.
5:     .DESCRIPTION
6:         Accepts a hashtable or PSCustomObject and saves it as JSON.
7:         Creates the config directory if it doesn't exist.
8:         Invalidates the config cache so subsequent reads use the new values.
9:     .PARAMETER Config
10:         Configuration object to save. Must be a hashtable or PSCustomObject.
11:     .EXAMPLE
12:         $config = Get-CFConfig
13:         $config.lolcat.enabled = $true
14:         Set-CFConfig -Config $config
15:     .EXAMPLE
16:         Set-CFConfig -Config @{ lolcat = @{ enabled = $true }; cow = @{ file = 'tux' } }
17:     #>
18:     [CmdletBinding(SupportsShouldProcess)]
19:     [OutputType([void])]
20:     param(
21:         [Parameter(Mandatory)]
22:         [ValidateNotNullOrEmpty()]
23:         [ValidateScript({ $_ -is [hashtable] -or $_ -is [PSCustomObject] })]
24:         $Config
25:     )
26: 
27:     $path = Get-ConfigPath
28:     $dir = Split-Path $path -Parent
29: 
30:     if (-not (Test-Path $dir)) {
31:         New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $dir -Force -ErrorAction Stop | Out-Null
32:     }
33: 
34:     if ($PSCmdlet.ShouldProcess($path, 'Save configuration')) {
35:         # Convert to JSON with sufficient depth
36:         $json = $Config | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 10
37: 
38:         # Atomic write: write to temp file then move (prevents corruption on crash)
39:         $tempPath = "$path.tmp"
40:         try {
41:             if (Test-Path $tempPath) { Remove-Item $tempPath -Force -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue }
42:             $json | Set-Content -Path $tempPath -Encoding UTF8 -Force -ErrorAction Stop
43:             if (Test-Path $path) { Remove-Item $path -Force -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue }
44:             Move-Item -Path $tempPath -Destination $path -Force -ErrorAction Stop
45:         }
46:         catch {
47:             if (Test-Path $tempPath) { Remove-Item $tempPath -Force -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue }
48:             throw
49:         }
50:     }
51: 
52:     # Invalidate cache
53:     $script:ConfigCache = $null
54:     $script:ConfigCacheTime = [datetime]::MinValue
55: }
```

```
<content>
1: function Read-CowFile {
2:     <#
3:     .SYNOPSIS
4:         Reads and parses a .cow template file with caching.
5:     .DESCRIPTION
6:         Extracts the $the_cow block from a Perl-format .cow file.
7:         Handles escape sequences (\@, \$, \\) and caches results for performance.
8:     #>
9:     [CmdletBinding()]
10:     param(
11:         [Parameter(Mandatory)]
12:         [string]$CowName,
13: 
14:         [string]$CustomPath
15:     )
16: 
17:     # Check cache first
18:     $cacheKey = if ($CustomPath) { $CustomPath } else { $CowName }
19:     if ($script:CowFileCache.ContainsKey($cacheKey)) {
20:         return $script:CowFileCache[$cacheKey]
21:     }
22: 
23:     # Resolve path
24:     if ($CustomPath) {
25:         $path = $CustomPath
26:     }
27:     else {
28:         $cowsPath = Join-Path (Split-Path $PSScriptRoot -Parent) 'Data/Cows'
29:         $path = Join-Path $cowsPath "$CowName.cow"
30:     }
31: 
32:     if (-not (Test-Path $path)) {
33:         throw "Cow file not found: $path"
34:     }
35: 
36:     $content = Get-Content $path -Raw -ErrorAction Stop
37:     $content = $content -replace "`r`n", "`n"
38: 
39:     # Extract $the_cow heredoc block
40:     # Use \n instead of \s* to preserve leading whitespace in cow template lines
41:     if ($content -match '(?s)\$the_cow\s*=\s*<<["'']?EOC["'']?;\n(.*?)\n\s*EOC') {
42:         $content = $Matches[1]
43:     }
44: 
45:     # Unescape Perl escape sequences (order matters: \\ before \@ and \$)
46:     $content = $content -replace '\\\\', '\'
47:     $content = $content -replace '\\@',  '@'
48:     $content = $content -replace '\\\$', '$'
49: 
50:     # Cache for subsequent calls
51:     $script:CowFileCache[$cacheKey] = $content
52: 
53:     return $content
54: }

(End of file - total 54 lines)
</content>
```

```
1: function Read-FortuneFile {

3:     .SYNOPSIS
4:         Reads and parses a fortune database file with caching.
5:     .DESCRIPTION
6:         Splits fortune file by % delimiters and returns an array of entries.
7:         Caches parsed results for performance.
8:     #>
9:     [CmdletBinding()]
10:     param(
11:         [Parameter(Mandatory)]
12:         [string]$Path
13:     )
14: 
15:     # Check cache first
16:     if ($script:FortuneCache.ContainsKey($Path)) {
17:         return $script:FortuneCache[$Path]
18:     }
19: 
20:     if (-not (Test-Path $Path)) {
21:         throw "Fortune file not found: $Path"

25:     $content = $content -replace '\r?\n', "`n"
```

```
4:         Returns a random fortune from the fortune database.
```

## Assistant (Build · MiMo V2.5 Free · 19.1s)

_Thinking:_

Now I have a thorough understanding of the entire codebase. Let me analyze the issues:

## CI Workflow Issues:
1. **No PowerShell version matrix** — only tests on latest pwsh, not PowerShell 5.1 (Windows) vs 7+
2. **No code coverage reporting** — can't track test coverage trends
3. **No module import stress test** — only imports once per test file
4. **No timeout on tests** — if an animation hangs, CI will run forever
5. **No artifact caching** — Pester/PSScriptAnalyzer reinstalled every run
6. **Build job doesn't validate the zip contents thoroughly**
7. **No security scan** — no SAST, no dependency scanning
8. **No performance benchmark** — no regression detection

## Test Rigor Issues:
1. **Animation tests don't verify output content** — only check `Should -Not -BeNullOrEmpty`, not that the cow face is present
2. **No cross-platform path tests** — config paths differ per OS but not tested
3. **No parallel execution test** — concurrent module imports
4. **No memory leak detection** — repeated calls could accumulate cache
5. **No timeout per test** — animations could hang
6. **Ghost tests don't test animation modes** — hostile QA missing new features
7. **No test for invalid animation mode** — what happens with `mode = 'invalid'`
8. **No test for config with new animation options** (blinkRate, amplitude) validation
9. **No test for concurrent config reads/writes**
10. **Fortune tests don't verify fortune count or content quality**

## Code Optimization Issues:
1. **Get-CFConfig** — the `$required` hashtable is recreated on every non-cached call. Should be a module-level constant.
2. **Read-FortuneFile** — splits entire file into array on every call (cached, but first call is expensive for 4000+ entries)
3. **Format-CowMessage** — uses string concatenation in loop instead of StringBuilder
4. **Lolcat Format-LolcatLine** — creates StringBuilder per line, could be optimized
5. **Animation functions** — some use `@()` array concatenation (`+=`) which creates new arrays each time (Dissolve uses this for PS 5.1 compat, but it's slow for large arrays)
6. **Show-Lolcat.ps1** — exists but appears unused (dead code?)

## UI/UX Issues:
1. **Talking animation** — the eye replacement regex `\\.*\([^)]{2}\)` may not match all cow formats
2. **Bounce animation** — gravity/damping values may need tuning for different terminal heights
3. **Wave animation** — balloon text extraction regex may fail on some cow formats
4. **Disco animation** — HSV calculation uses uninitialized `$r`, `$g`, `$b` variables in default case

Let me now fix these issues systematically.

Now I have a complete picture. Let me fix all issues systematically:

```json
  "content": "name: CI\n\non:\n  push:\n    branches: [main]\n    tags: ['v*']\n  pull_request:\n    branches: [main]\n\nenv:\n  MODULE_NAME: Forgum\n\njobs:\n  lint:\n    runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n ## User
```

see if cpp, rust , or ruby is required to make the program more easily I would appreciate to start it soon and integrate with powershell only if its easy and more better than existing in all aspect.

## Assistant (Build · MiMo V2.5 Free · 27.9s)

_Thinking:_

The user is asking me to evaluate whether C++, Rust, or Ruby would be beneficial to integrate with the PowerShell-based Forgum project. Let me think about this carefully.

Current state: Forgum is a pure PowerShell module with 195 tests, 11 animation modes, 107 cow files, fortune system, lolcat colorization, and cross-platform support.

Let me analyze each language:

**C++:**
- Could be used for a native binary that handles the animation rendering loop
- Would be MUCH faster for the animation frame rendering (disco, dissolve, etc.)
- But: Requires compilation, platform-specific builds, adds complexity
- PowerShell can call native executables via `Start-Process` or `&`
- Overkill for what Forgum does — the bottleneck is `Start-Sleep`, not computation

**Rust:**
- Similar to C++ but memory-safe
- Could create a fast CLI tool
- But: Same compilation/build concerns
- PowerShell module is already cross-platform via pwsh
- No real performance bottleneck that needs Rust

**Ruby:**
- Cowsay originally IS a Ruby script
- But: Adds a runtime dependency (Ruby must be installed)
- PowerShell already handles everything Ruby would do
- No advantage over existing PowerShell implementation

**My assessment:**
None of these languages are needed. The current PowerShell implementation is:
1. Already cross-platform (Windows/macOS/Linux via pwsh)
2. Already fast enough (animations run smoothly)
3. Already has 195 passing tests
4. Already has no external dependencies beyond PowerShell

The only potential benefit would be C++/Rust for a native binary that could be distributed without PowerShell — but that defeats the purpose of being a PowerShell module.

However, there are 2 failing tests I should fix first:
1. "config path is valid for current platform" — `Get-ConfigPath` is a private function not exported, so it's not accessible in tests
2. "config directory parent exists or can be created" — same issue

Let me fix these test failures and then address the user's question.

Actually, looking more carefully at the test failures:
```
Failed: {[-] config path is valid for current platform, [-] config directory parent exists or can be created}
```

These are in the "Cross-Platform" describe block. The issue is that `Get-ConfigPath` is a private function — it's dot-sourced into the module scope but not exported. In Pester, when you import the module, private functions are available within the module's scope but not in the test's scope directly.

Wait, actually dot-sourced functions should be available after Import-Module. Let me check... The functions are dot-sourced in Forgum.psm1, so they should be available in the module scope. But when calling from test script, you need to use `InModuleScope` or the function needs to be exported.

Actually, looking at the error more carefully — the tests are calling `Get-ConfigPath` directly. Since it's a private function (not in the FunctionsToExport), it won't be available in the test scope. I need to either:
1. Export it (not ideal for a private function)
2. Use `InModuleScope` in the tests
3. Test the config path indirectly

Let me fix this by using InModuleScope or by testing the path through the public API.

Actually, the simplest fix is to just test the config behavior through Get-CFConfig and Set-CFConfig, which are public functions. Or I can use InModuleScope.

Let me fix the test failures and address the user's question.

Two failing tests to fix first, then I'll address the language question.

The failures are because `Get-ConfigPath` is a private function not exported. Let me fix:

**Tool: edit**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "D:\\Projects\\Forgum\\Tests\\Forgum.Tests.ps1",
  "newString": "Describe \"Cross-Platform\" {\n    BeforeAll {\n        Import-Module (Join-Path (Split-Path $PSScriptRoot -Parent) 'Forgum.psd1') -Force\n    }\n\n    It \"config path is valid for current platform\" {\n        $path = InModuleScope Forgum { Get-ConfigPath }\n        $path | Should -Not -BeNullOrEmpty\n        $path | Should -Match 'config\\.json$'\n    }\n\n    It \"config directory parent exists or can be created\" {\n        $path = InModuleScope Forgum { Get-ConfigPath }\n        $dir = Split-Path $path -Parent\n        $dir | Should -Not -BeNullOrEmpty\n    }",
  "oldString": "Describe \"Cross-Platform\" {\n    BeforeAll {\n        Import-Module (Join-Path (Split-Path $PSScriptRoot -Parent) 'Forgum.psd1') -Force\n    }\n\n    It \"config path is valid for current platform\" {\n        $path = Get-ConfigPath\n        $path | Should -Not -BeNullOrEmpty\n        $path | Should -Match 'config\\.json$'\n    }\n\n    It \"config directory parent exists or can be created\" {\n        $path = Get-ConfigPath\n        $dir = Split-Path $path -Parent\n        $dir | Should -Not -BeNullOrEmpty\n    }"
}
```

- **Module-level constants for performance**: `$script:DefaultConfigSections` avoids per-call hashtable allocation

Let me update the anchored summary based on the new conversation history. Key changes:

1. User asked whether C++, Rust, or Ruby would be useful to integrate with Forgum

   - Cross-Platform BeforeAll: Added `Remove-Module Forgum -Force` before re-importing to avoid "Multiple script or manifest modules" error
   - Version comparison: Cast to `[string]` to avoid array comparison issues

## Key Decisions
- **Auto-start uses static mode**: Prevents double-output (animation Write-Host + string return printed again)
- **Talking animation no longer uses Clear-Host**: Cursor repositioning for smooth frames
- **Scoop via personal bucket `hkdevloops/forgum`**: User has `HKDevLoops` org on GitHub
- **Winget kept**: User confirmed winget doesn't require 100 stars
- **Animation + Lolcat integration**: `Invoke-Forgum` renders cow WITHOUT lolcat first, runs animation, then applies lolcat after
- **Config reset via template file**: `Get-Content .../default-config.json | ConvertFrom-Json` in BeforeAll
- **Module-level constants for performance**: `$script:DefaultConfigSections` avoids per-call hashtable allocation
- **PS 5.1 compatibility**: Dissolve uses nested `@()` arrays; Blink uses `@()` instead of `[System.Collections.Generic.List[int]]::new()`
- **CI matrix**: pwsh 7.4 on all 3 OS + pwsh 5.1 on Windows-only
- **Private functions in tests require InModuleScope**: `Get-ConfigPath` is private, accessed via `InModuleScope Forgum { Get-ConfigPath }`
- **C++/Rust/Ruby not needed**: PowerShell is sufficient for all Forgum's requirements (cross-platform, animations, tests, no compute bottleneck requiring native code)

```
1: function Show-CFAnimation {
2:     <#
3:     .SYNOPSIS
4:         Displays cow output with the configured animation mode.
5:     .DESCRIPTION
6:         Dispatches to the appropriate animation function based on config.
7:         Modes: static, talking, typewriter, slide-in, bounce, dissolve,
8:         fade-in, blink, wiggle, wave, disco.
9:     .PARAMETER CowOutput
10:         The rendered cow string to animate.
11:     .PARAMETER Message
12:         The original message text (used by some animations).
13:     .EXAMPLE
14:         Show-CFAnimation -CowOutput $cow -Message "Hello"
15:     #>
16:     [CmdletBinding()]
17:     [OutputType([string])]
18:     param(
19:         [Parameter(Mandatory)]
20:         [string]$CowOutput,
21: 
22:         [string]$Message = ''
23:     )
24: 
25:     $config = Get-CFConfig
26:     $mode = $config.animation.mode
27: 
28:     switch ($mode) {
29:         'talking' {
30:             return Invoke-TalkingAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Duration $config.animation.duration
31:         }
32:         'typewriter' {
33:             return Invoke-TypewriterAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Speed $config.animation.speed
34:         }
35:         'slide-in' {
36:             return Invoke-SlideInAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Speed $config.animation.speed
37:         }
38:         'bounce' {
39:             return Invoke-BounceAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Duration $config.animation.duration
40:         }
41:         'dissolve' {
42:             return Invoke-DissolveAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Duration $config.animation.duration
43:         }
44:         'fade-in' {
45:             return Invoke-FadeInAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Duration $config.animation.duration
46:         }
47:         'blink' {
48:             return Invoke-BlinkAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Duration $config.animation.duration -BlinkRate $config.animation.blinkRate
49:         }
50:         'wiggle' {
51:             return Invoke-WiggleAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Duration $config.animation.duration -Amplitude $config.animation.amplitude
52:         }
53:         'wave' {
54:             return Invoke-WaveAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Speed $config.animation.speed
55:         }
56:         'disco' {
57:             return Invoke-DiscoAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message -Speed $config.animation.speed -Duration $config.animation.duration
58:         }
59:         default {
60:             return Invoke-StaticAnimation -CowOutput $CowOutput -Message $Message
61:         }
```

## Assistant (Build · Nemotron 3 Ultra Free · 109.2s)

_Thinking:_

The user wants a new "dynamic" animation mode that cycles through different animals (cows) and different fortunes/thoughts. Let me create this new animation mode. It should:
1. Pick a random cow
2. Pick a random fortune
3. Display it with some animation
4. After a delay, transition to another cow/fortune
5. Keep cycling

Let me create this new animation file and add it to the dispatcher.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "D:\\Projects\\Forgum\\Private\\Animation\\Dynamic.ps1",
  "content": "function Invoke-DynamicAnimation {\n    <#\n    .SYNOPSIS\n        Cycles through random animals and fortunes continuously.\n    .DESCRIPTION\n        Picks a random cow and random fortune, displays with a brief\n        transition animation, then cycles to the next pair. Runs for\n        the configured duration.\n    .PARAMETER CowOutput\n        Ignored - generates fresh cow+fortune each cycle.\n    .PARAMETER Message\n        Ignored - uses random fortunes.\n    .PARAMETER Duration\n        Total animation duration in seconds (default 10).\n    .PARAMETER CycleInterval\n        Seconds between each cow/fortune change (default 3).\n    #>\n    [CmdletBinding()]\n    [OutputType([string])]\n    param(\n        [string]$CowOutput = '',\n        [string]$Message = '',\n        [double]$Duration = 10,\n        [double]$CycleInterval = 3\n    )\n\n    $config = Get-CFConfig\n    $cowsPath = Join-Path $PSScriptRoot '..\\..\\Data\\Cows'\n    $fortunesPath = Join-Path $PSScriptRoot '..\\..\\Data\\Fortunes\\fortunes.txt'\n    \n    $cowFiles = Get-ChildItem -Path $cowsPath -Filter '*.cow' | Select-Object -ExpandProperty FullName\n    $fortunes = Get-Content $fortunesPath -Raw -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue\n    $fortuneList = if ($fortunes) { $fortunes -split '(?m)^%\\s*$' | Where-Object { $_.Trim() } } else { @() }\n\n    if (-not $cowFiles -or -not $fortuneList) {\n        return \"No cows or fortunes available\"\n    }\n\n    $startTime = [DateTime]::UtcNow\n    $endTime = $startTime.AddSeconds($Duration)\n    $frameDelay = 50\n    $lastCycle = $startTime\n    $currentCow = ''\n    $currentFortune = ''\n    $firstRun = $true\n\n    try {\n        while ([DateTime]::UtcNow -lt $endTime) {\n            $now = [DateTime]::UtcNow\n            $elapsed = ($now - $startTime).TotalSeconds\n            $shouldCycle = ($now - $lastCycle).TotalSeconds -ge $CycleInterval -or $firstRun\n\n            if ($shouldCycle) {\n                $currentCow = Get-Content ($cowFiles | Get-Random) -Raw\n                $currentFortune = $fortuneList | Get-Random\n                $lastCycle = $now\n                $firstRun = $false\n            }\n\n            $cowLines = $currentCow -split \"`r?`n\"\n            $fortuneLines = $currentFortune.Trim() -split \"`r?`n\"\n            \n            $maxWidth = ($cowLines | Measure-Object -Property Length -Maximum).Maximum\n            $fortuneLines | ForEach-Object { if ($_.Length -gt $maxWidth) { $maxWidth = $_.Length } }\n            $balloonWidth = [math]::Max($maxWidth, 40)\n\n            $top = ' ' + ('-' * ($balloonWidth + 2))\n            $bottom = ' ' + ('-' * ($balloonWidth + 2))\n            $balloon = @()\n            $balloon += $top\n            foreach ($line in $fortuneLines) {\n                $pad = $balloonWidth - $line.Length\n                $balloon += \"| $line$(' ' * $pad) |\"\n            }\n            $balloon += $bottom\n            $balloon += $cowLines\n\n            $output = $balloon -join \"`n\"\n            \n            if ($config.lolcat.enabled -and (Get-Command lolcat -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue)) {\n                $output = $output | Format-Lolcat\n            }\n\n            $cursorPos = [Console]::CursorTop\n            if ($cursorPos -gt 0) {\n                [Console]::SetCursorPosition(0, $cursorPos - $balloon.Count)\n            }\n            Write-Host $output -NoNewline\n\n            Start-Sleep -Milliseconds $frameDelay\n        }\n    }\n    finally {\n        Write-Host \"\"\n    }\n\n    return $output\n}"
}
```
